 				$('.ui-corner-top', this).removeClass('ui-corner-top');
 			},
 			hide: {
 				effect: "fade",
 				duration: 250
 			},
 			show: {
 				effect: "fade",
 				duration: 250
 			},
 			activate: function (event, ui) {
 				var sliderClassName = ui.newPanel.attr('id');
 				if ( sliderClassName.indexOf("fragment-ad") > -1 ) {
 					$("#nfy-cobo-5b616ea07eda5 .nfy-arrow-left").hide();
 					$("#nfy-cobo-5b616ea07eda5 .nfy-arrow-right").hide();
 				}
 				else {
 					$("#nfy-cobo-5b616ea07eda5 .nfy-arrow-left").show();
 					$("#nfy-cobo-5b616ea07eda5 .nfy-arrow-right").show();
 				}
 			}
 		});
 
 		counter_5b616ea07eda5 = 0;
 		autorotate_featured_ar_teaser_5b616ea07eda5 = true;
 		max_index_5b616ea07eda5 = parseInt(jQuery("#nfy-cobo-5b616ea07eda5 ul.nfy-cobo-ui-tabs-nav>li").filter(function () {
 					if ( jQuery(this).css('visibility') === 'visible' ) {
 						return true;
 					}
 					return false;
 				}).length) - 1;
 
 		requestInterval(function () {
 			if ( counter_5b616ea07eda5 > max_index_5b616ea07eda5 * 10 ) {
 				counter_5b616ea07eda5 = counter_5b616ea07eda5 % (max_index_5b616ea07eda5 + 1);
 			}
 
 			if ( autorotate_featured_ar_teaser_5b616ea07eda5 ) {
 				max_index_5b616ea07eda5 = parseInt(jQuery("#nfy-cobo-5b616ea07eda5 ul.nfy-cobo-ui-tabs-nav>li").filter(function () {
 							if ( jQuery(this).css('visibility') === 'visible' ) {
 								return true;
 							}
 							return false;
 						}).length) - 1;
 
 				$("#nfy-cobo-5b616ea07eda5").tabs("option", "active", ++counter_5b616ea07eda5 % (max_index_5b616ea07eda5 + 1));
 			}
 		}, 10000);
 
 		$("#nfy-cobo-5b616ea07eda5 .nfy-arrow-right").click(function () {
 			$("#nfy-cobo-5b616ea07eda5").tabs("option", "active", (++counter_5b616ea07eda5 % (max_index_5b616ea07eda5 + 1)));
 		});
 
 		$("#nfy-cobo-5b616ea07eda5 .nfy-arrow-left").click(function () {
 			$("#nfy-cobo-5b616ea07eda5").tabs("option", "active", (--counter_5b616ea07eda5 % (max_index_5b616ea07eda5 + 1)));
 		});
 
 		$("#nfy-cobo-5b616ea07eda5").swipe({
 			excludedElements: "button, input, select, textarea, .noSwipe",

 			},

 				$("#nfy-cobo-5b616ea07eda5").tabs("option", "active", (--counter_5b616ea07eda5 % (max_index_5b616ea07eda5 + 1)));

 jQuery(document).ready(function($){
 	$("#nfy-cobo-5b616db660713").tabs({
 		event: "mouseover",
 		fx:{
 			opacity: "toggle",
 			duration: "medium"
 		},
 		create: function(event, ui) {
 			$('.ui-corner-top', this).removeClass('ui-corner-top');
 		},
 		hide: {
 			effect: "fade",
 			duration: 250
 		},
 		show: {
 			effect: "fade",
 			duration: 250
 		},
 		activate: function(event, ui) {
 			var sliderClassName = ui.newPanel.attr('class');
 			if( sliderClassName.indexOf("fragment--ad") > -1 )
 			{
 				$("#nfy-cobo-5b616db660713 .nfy-arrow-left").hide();
 				$("#nfy-cobo-5b616db660713 .nfy-arrow-right").hide();
 			}
 			else
 			{
 				$("#nfy-cobo-5b616db660713 .nfy-arrow-left").show();
 				$("#nfy-cobo-5b616db660713 .nfy-arrow-right").show();
 			}
 		}
 	});
 
 	counter_5b616db660713 = 0;
 	autorotate_featured_ar_teaser_5b616db660713 = true;
 	max_index_5b616db660713 = parseInt(jQuery("#nfy-cobo-5b616db660713 .nfy-cobo-ui-tabs-nav li").length)-1;
 
 	requestInterval(function() {
 		if( counter_5b616db660713 > max_index_5b616db660713 * 10 )
 		{
 			counter_5b616db660713 = counter_5b616db660713 % (max_index_5b616db660713+1);
 		}
 
 		if(autorotate_featured_ar_teaser_5b616db660713)
 		{
 			$( "#nfy-cobo-5b616db660713" ).tabs( "option", "active", ++counter_5b616db660713 % (max_index_5b616db660713+1));
 		}
 	}, 11000);
 
 	$("#nfy-cobo-5b616db660713 .nfy-arrow-right").click(function() {
 		$( "#nfy-cobo-5b616db660713" ).tabs( "option", "active", (++counter_5b616db660713 % (max_index_5b616db660713+1)));
 	});
 
 	$("#nfy-cobo-5b616db660713 .nfy-arrow-left").click(function() {
 		$( "#nfy-cobo-5b616db660713" ).tabs( "option", "active", (--counter_5b616db660713 % (max_index_5b616db660713+1)));
 	});
 
 	$("#nfy-cobo-5b616db660713").swipe({
 		excludedElements: "button, input, select, textarea, .noSwipe",
 		swipeLeft: function() {
 			$( "#nfy-cobo-5b616db660713" ).tabs( "option", "active", (++counter_5b616db660713 % (max_index_5b616db660713+1)));

 	jQuery(document).ready(function($){
 		$("#nfy-cobo-5b616dba9a9d0").tabs({
 			/*heightStyle: "auto",*/
 			event: "mouseover",
 			fx:{
 				opacity: "toggle",
 				duration: "medium"
 			},
 			create: function(event, ui) {
 				$('.ui-corner-top', this).removeClass('ui-corner-top');
 			},
 			hide: {
 				effect: "fade",
 				duration: 250
 			},
 			show: {
 				effect: "fade",
 				duration: 250
 			},
 			activate: function(event, ui) {
 				var sliderClassName = ui.newPanel.attr('class');
 				if( sliderClassName.indexOf("fragment--ad") > -1 )
 				{
 					$("#nfy-cobo-5b616dba9a9d0 .nfy-arrow-left").hide();
 					$("#nfy-cobo-5b616dba9a9d0 .nfy-arrow-right").hide();
 				}
 				else
 				{
 					$("#nfy-cobo-5b616dba9a9d0 .nfy-arrow-left").show();
 					$("#nfy-cobo-5b616dba9a9d0 .nfy-arrow-right").show();
 				}
 			}
 		});
 
 		counter_5b616dba9a9d0 = 0;
 		autorotate_featured_ar_teaser_5b616dba9a9d0 = true;
 		max_index_5b616dba9a9d0 = parseInt(jQuery("#nfy-cobo-5b616dba9a9d0 ul.nfy-cobo-ui-tabs-nav>li").filter(function() {
 			if( jQuery(this).css('visibility') === 'visible' )
 			{
 				return true;
 			}
 			return false;
 		}).length)-1;
 
 		requestInterval(function() {
 			if( counter_5b616dba9a9d0 > max_index_5b616dba9a9d0 * 10 )
 			{
 				counter_5b616dba9a9d0 = counter_5b616dba9a9d0 % (max_index_5b616dba9a9d0+1);
 			}
 
 			if(autorotate_featured_ar_teaser_5b616dba9a9d0)
 			{
 				max_index_5b616dba9a9d0 = parseInt(jQuery("#nfy-cobo-5b616dba9a9d0 ul.nfy-cobo-ui-tabs-nav>li").filter(function() {
 					if( jQuery(this).css('visibility') === 'visible' )
 					{
 						return true;
 					}
 					return false;
 				}).length)-1;
 
 				$( "#nfy-cobo-5b616dba9a9d0" ).tabs( "option", "active", ++counter_5b616dba9a9d0 % (max_index_5b616dba9a9d0+1));
 			}
 		}, 10000);
 
 		$("#nfy-cobo-5b616dba9a9d0 .nfy-arrow-right").click(function() {
 			$( "#nfy-cobo-5b616dba9a9d0" ).tabs( "option", "active", (++counter_5b616dba9a9d0 % (max_index_5b616dba9a9d0+1)));
 		});
 
 		$("#nfy-cobo-5b616dba9a9d0 .nfy-arrow-left").click(function() {
 			$( "#nfy-cobo-5b616dba9a9d0" ).tabs( "option", "active", (--counter_5b616dba9a9d0 % (max_index_5b616dba9a9d0+1)));
 		});
 
 		$("#nfy-cobo-5b616dba9a9d0").swipe({
 			excludedElements: "button, input, select, textarea, .noSwipe",
 			swipeLeft: function() {
 				$( "#nfy-cobo-5b616dba9a9d0" ).tabs( "option", "active", (++counter_5b616dba9a9d0 % (max_index_5b616dba9a9d0+1)));
 			},
 			swipeRight: function() {
 				$( "#nfy-cobo-5b616dba9a9d0" ).tabs( "option", "active", (--counter_5b616dba9a9d0 % (max_index_5b616dba9a9d0+1)));
 			},
 			allowPageScroll: 'vertical'
 		});
 	});
 	/*  */
       </script>
